   <script>
    var $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {};
 
     jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
 
         $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {
 
             facebookPixel: null,
             customEvent: false,
             pixelFired: false,
             events: {
                 EPrice: {
                     name: "EPrice",
                     type: "click",
                     value: ".results_table .primary-cta .button-form, #details-page-ctabox .maincta-row .button-form, .cta-box .vdp-primary.button-form, #cta-mobile-button"
                 },
                 SRP: {
                     name: "SRP",
                     type: "element",
                     value: $(".page-vehicle-results-page")
                 },
                 VDP: {
                     name: "VDP",
                     type: "element",
                     value: $(".page-vehicle-display-page")
                 },
                 Lead: {
                     name: "Lead",
                     type: "url",
                     value: "thank-you"
                 },
                 Parts: {
                     name: "Parts",
                     type: "url",
                     value: "parts"
                 },
                 Service: {
                     name: "Service",
                     type: "url",
                     value:"service"
                 }
             },
 
             init: function() {
                 this.checkCustomEvents();
             },
 
             checkCustomEvents: function() {
                 var self = this;
                 for(eventName in self.events) {
                     if(!self.customEvent) {
                         switch(self.events[eventName].type) {
                             case "element":
                                 if(
                                     typeof self.events[eventName].value !== "undefined"
                                     &&
                                     self.events[eventName].value.length > 0
                                 )
                                     self.customEvent = eventName;
 
                                 break;
                             case "url":
                                 var url = location.href;
                                 var searchString = new RegExp(self.events[eventName].value, "g");
                                 if(url.search(searchString) !== -1)
                                     self.customEvent = eventName;
                                 break;
                             case "click":
                                 var clickEvent = eventName;
                                 $("body").on('click', self.events[eventName].value, function(e) {
                                     var customData = $(e.target).data("vehicle");
                                     console.log(e.target, "The above element was clicked, which sends this FB Remarketing Event: '" + clickEvent + "'");
                                     fbq('trackCustom', clickEvent, customData);
                                 });
                                 break;
                         }
                     }
                 }
 
                 self.fireFacebookEvents();
             },
 
             fireFacebookEvents: function() {
                 var self = this;
 
                 // Enqueue the `fbevents.js` script
                 self.facebookPixels = ["852303121569558"];
                 !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s)
                 {if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
                 n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
                 if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
                 n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
                 t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
                 s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
                 'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');
 
                 // Create the `fqb` event
                 for(pixel in self.facebookPixels) {
                     fbq('init', self.facebookPixels[pixel]);
                 }
                 // Handle any found custom events
                 if(self.customEvent) {
                     console.log("FB Remarketing Event: '" + self.customEvent + "'");
                     if(self.customEvent == "VDP" && typeof inventory_localization == "object") {
                         var customData = inventory_localization.vehicle;
                         fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent, customData);
                         
                     } else {
                         fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent);
                     }
                     
                     self.pixelFired = true;
                     
                 }
                 // Send the pageview
                 fbq('track', 'PageView');
             }
         };

         <p>
          Butler Collision Centers are part of the Butler Automotive Group which has been operating in the middle Georgia area for over 40 yrs.           The bottom line for our customers is that we are able to perform the highest-quality collision repairs. There are several reasons for this.  First, we have the best equipment, including the most modern frame and alignment machines. Second, the size of the shop gives our technicians plenty of room to work. Our technicians are trained and certified by Toyota. Our computerized paint mixing system, and paint booths ensure that your paint will match the factory paint.

Although we are proud of the quality of our repairs, we are even more proud of what our customers have to say about our work. We work on all makes and models of vehicles and work with all major insurance companies. Remember, you have the right to choose where your vehicle is repaired. If you need collision repair, paint work, or just a good detail, please visit us and give us the opportunity to show you what we can do.

         <p>
          Since 1970, Butler Toyota has been a family-owned-and-operated dealership that has proudly helped drivers in the Macon, Warner Robins, and Milledgeville areas find a vehicle that they can absolutely rely on. Our goal is provide drivers with a fun, unique, and memorable experience when they’re actively seeking out their next car. When you decide it’s time to start looking for your next car, we’ll be happy to help you every step of the way, from when you arrive on our lot until we’re waving goodbye as you’re making your way home in your new Toyota.

          </strong>

          <a href="//macon.butlertoyota.com/new-vehicles/">

 (function($,window){function isMobile(){return window.innerWidth<767}

 function pauseVideoSlide(slide){if(slide.type!="video"){return}
 if(slide.player){slide.player.pauseVideo()}}
 function playVideoSlide(slide,swiper){if(slide.type!="video"){return}

 setTimeout(function(){if(event.target&&slide.active){playVideoSlide(slide,swiper)}},duration)}
 if(event.data===YT.PlayerState.ENDED){if(typeof swiper!='undefined'){swiper.slideNext();swiper.autoplay.start();return}}}}else{if(!slide.videoSlideNext){if(event.data===YT.PlayerState.ENDED){var seekToTime=(typeof slide.videoStart!='defined'&&slide.videoStart)?slide.videoStart:0;slide.player.seekTo(seekToTime)
 slide.player.playVideo()}}}}}})
 function maybeTransitionVideoSlide(){var playerState=slide.player.getPlayerState()
